                   </div>
                   <!-- end ngIf: goSlow -->

                   <div class="ng-binding ng-scope" ng-bind="::goSlow ? 'Say what?' : 'Go faster'" ng-if="true || !haveScrolled || isHovered">

                   </div>
                   <!-- end ngIf: true || !haveScrolled || isHovered -->

                   <div aria-hidden="true" class="ng-hide flex" flex="" ng-show="isHovered">

                     help

                 <div class="page-title md-display-3">

                    <arb-page-title class="ng-isolate-scope" is-link="true" page-id="1zg">
                     <!-- ngIf: ::(showType && page.type === 'question') -->

                     Bayes' rule: Vector form
                     <!-- end ngIf: ::isLink -->
                     <!-- ngIf: ::!isLink -->
                     <!-- ngIf: ::showClickbait -->
                    </arb-page-title>
                   </span>
                   <!-- end ngRepeat: subject in page.subjects | orderBy: ['-isStrong', '-level'] -->
                   <span class="ng-scope" ng-repeat="subject in page.subjects | orderBy: ['-isStrong', '-level']">
                    <!-- ngIf: ::$index > 0 && $index < page.subjects.length -->

                     ,
                    </span>
                    <!-- end ngIf: ::$index > 0 && $index < page.subjects.length -->
                    <arb-page-title class="ng-isolate-scope" is-link="true" page-id="1rj">
                     <!-- ngIf: ::(showType && page.type === 'question') -->
                     <!-- ngIf: ::isLink -->
                     Conditional probability
                     <!-- end ngIf: ::isLink -->
                     <!-- ngIf: ::!isLink -->
                     <!-- ngIf: ::showClickbait -->
                    </arb-page-title>

                   <!-- end ngRepeat: subject in page.subjects | orderBy: ['-isStrong', '-level'] -->
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <!-- end ngIf: page.requirements.length > 0 || page.subjects.length > 0 -->
                 <!-- ngIf: ::page.text.length > 0 -->
                 <md-progress-linear aria-valuemax="100" aria-valuemin="0" class="ng-scope" md-mode="query" role="progressbar">
                  <div class="md-container md-mode-query">
                   <div class="md-dashed">
                   </div>
                   <div class="md-bar md-bar1">
                   </div>
                   <div class="md-bar md-bar2">
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </md-progress-linear>
                 <arb-markdown class="lens-text ng-scope ng-isolate-scope markdown-text invisible" ng-if="::page.text.length &gt; 0" page-id="693">
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   (This is a high-speed introduction to
                   Bayes' rule
                   for people who want to get straight to it and are good at math.  If you'd like a gentler or more thorough introduction, try starting at the
                   Bayes' Rule Guide
                   page instead.)
                  </p>
                  <h1 class="ng-scope">
                   Percentages, frequencies, and waterfalls
                  </h1>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Suppose you're screening a set of patients for a disease, which we'll call Diseasitis.
                   <span arb-text-popover-anchor="" class="markdown-note ng-isolate-scope" encoded-html="Lit.%20%22inflammation%20of%20the%20disease%22." replacement-text="1">
                    1
                   </span>
                   Your initial test is a tongue depressor containing a chemical strip, which usually turns black if the patient has Diseasitis.
                  </p>
                  <ul class="ng-scope">
                   <li>
                    Based on prior epidemiology, you expect that around 20% of patients in the screening population have Diseasitis.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Among patients with Diseasitis, 90% turn the tongue depressor black.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    30% of the patients without Diseasitis will also turn the tongue depressor black.
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   What fraction of patients with black tongue depressors have Diseasitis?
                  </p>
                  <div arb-hidden-text="" button-text="Answer" class="ng-scope ng-isolate-scope">
                   <button aria-label="Answer" class="md-primary md-hue-1 md-raised md-button ng-binding ng-scope md-ink-ripple" ng-bind="buttonText" ng-click="toggle()" ng-transclude="" type="button">
                    Answer
                   </button>
                   <div class="hidden-text display-none">
                    <p>
                     3/7 or 43%, quickly obtainable as follows:  In the screened population, there's 1 sick patient for 4 healthy patients.  Sick patients are 3 times more likely to turn the tongue depressor black than healthy patients.
                     <span arb-math-compiler="$(1%20%3A%204)%20%5Ccdot%20(3%20%3A%201)%20%3D%20(3%20%3A%204)$">
                      <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                       <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-1">
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-2" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                         (
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-3">
                         1
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-4" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                         :
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-5">
                         4
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-6" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                         )
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-7" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                         ⋅
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-8" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                         (
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-9">
                         3
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-10" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                         :
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-11">
                         1
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-12" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                         )
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-13" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                         =
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-14" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                         (
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-15">
                         3
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-16" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                         :
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-17">
                         4
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-18" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                         )
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <script id="MathJax-Element-1" type="math/tex">
                       (1 : 4) \cdot (3 : 1) = (3 : 4)
                      </script>
                     </span>
                     or 3 sick patients to 4 healthy patients among those that turn the tongue depressor black, corresponding to a probability of
                     <span arb-math-compiler="$3%2F7%20%3D%2043%5C%25$">
                      <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                       <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-19">
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-20">
                         3
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-21">
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-22" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.111em;">
                          /
                         </span>
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-23">
                         7
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-24" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                         =
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-25">
                         43
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mi" id="MJXp-Span-26">
                         %
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <script id="MathJax-Element-2" type="math/tex">
                       3/7 = 43\%
                      </script>
                     </span>
                     that the patient is sick.
                    </p>
                   </div>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                  </div>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   (Take your own stab at answering this question, then please click "Answer" above to read the answer before continuing.)
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Bayes' rule is a theorem which describes the general form of the operation we carried out to find the answer above.  In the form we used above, we:
                  </p>
                  <ul class="ng-scope">
                   <li>
                    Started from the
                    <em>
                     prior odds
                    </em>
                    of (1 : 4) for sick versus healthy patients;
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Multiplied by the
                    <em>
                     likelihood ratio
                    </em>
                    of (3 : 1) for sick versus healthy patients blackening the tongue depressor;
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Arrived at
                    <em>
                     posterior odds
                    </em>
                    of (3 : 4) for a patient with a positive test result being sick versus healthy.
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Bayes' rule in this form thus states that
                   <strong>
                    the prior odds times the likelihood ratio equals the posterior odds.
                   </strong>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   We could also potentially see the positive test result as
                   <strong>
                    revising
                   </strong>
                   a
                   <em>
                    prior belief
                   </em>
                   or
                   <em>
                    prior probability
                   </em>
                   of 20% that the patient was sick, to a
                   <em>
                    posterior belief
                   </em>
                   or
                   <em>
                    posterior probability
                   </em>
                   of 43%.
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   To make it clearer that we did the correct calculation above, and further pump intuitions for Bayes' rule, we'll walk through some additional visualizations.
                  </p>
                  <h2 class="ng-scope">
                   Frequency representation
                  </h2>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   The
                   <em>
                    frequency representation
                   </em>
                   of Bayes' rule would describe the problem as follows:  "Among 100 patients, there will be 20 sick patients and 80 healthy patients."
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <img alt="prior frequency" src="https://i.imgur.com/gvcoqQN.png?0" title=""/>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   "18 out of 20 sick patients will turn the tongue depressor black.  24 out of 80 healthy patients will blacken the tongue depressor."
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <img alt="posterior frequency" src="https://i.imgur.com/0XDbrYi.png?0" title=""/>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   "Therefore, there are (18+24)=42 patients who turn the tongue depressor black, among whom 18 are actually sick. (18/42)=(3/7)=43%."
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   (Some experiments show
                   <span arb-text-popover-anchor="" class="markdown-note ng-isolate-scope" encoded-html="E.g.%20%22%3Ca%20href%3D%22https%3A%2F%2Ffaculty.washington.edu%2Fjmiyamot%2Fp548%2Feddydm%2520prob%2520reas%2520i%2520clin%2520medicine.pdf%22%3EProbabilistic%20reasoning%20in%20clinical%20medicine%3C%2Fa%3E%22%20by%20David%20M.%20Eddy%20(1982)." replacement-text="2">
                    2
                   </span>
                   that this way of explaining the problem is the easiest for e.g. medical students to understand, so you may want to remember this format for future use.  Assuming you can't just send them to Arbital!)
                  </p>
                  <h2 class="ng-scope">
                   Waterfall representation
                  </h2>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   The
                   <em>
                    waterfall representation
                   </em>
                   may make clearer why we're also allowed to transform the problem into prior odds and a likelihood ratio, and multiply (1 : 4) by (3 : 1) to get posterior odds of (3 : 4) and a probability of 3/7.
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   The following problem is isomorphic to the Diseasitis one:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   "A waterfall has two streams of water at the top, a red stream and a blue stream.  These streams flow down the waterfall, with some of each stream being diverted off to the side, and the remainder pools at the bottom of the waterfall."
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <img alt="unlabeled waterfall" src="https://i.imgur.com/D8EhY65.png?0" title=""/>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   "At the top of the waterfall, there's around 20 gallons/second flowing from the red stream, and 80 gallons/second flowing from the blue stream.  90% of the red water makes it to the bottom of the waterfall, and 30% of the blue water makes it to the bottom of the waterfall.  Of the purplish water that mixes at the bottom, what fraction is from the red stream versus the blue stream?"
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <img alt="labeled waterfall" src="https://i.imgur.com/QIrtuVU.png?0" title=""/>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   We can see from staring at the diagram that the
                   <em>
                    prior odds
                   </em>
                   and
                   <em>
                    likelihood ratio
                   </em>
                   are the only numbers we need to arrive at the answer:
                  </p>
                  <ul class="ng-scope">
                   <li>
                    The problem would have the same answer if there were 40 gallons/sec of red water and 160 gallons/sec of blue water (instead of 20 gallons/sec and 80 gallons/sec).  This would just multiply the total amount of water by a factor of 2, without changing the ratio of red to blue at the bottom.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    The problem would also have the same answer if 45% of the red stream and 15% of the blue stream made it to the bottom (instead of 90% and 30%).  This would just cut down the total amount of water by a factor of 2, without changing the
                    <em>
                     relative
                    </em>
                    proportions of red and blue water.
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <img alt="wide vs narrow waterfall" src="https://i.imgur.com/6FOndjc.png?0" title=""/>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   So only the
                   <em>
                    ratio
                   </em>
                   of red to blue water at the top (prior odds of the proposition), and only the
                   <em>
                    ratio
                   </em>
                   between the percentages of red and blue water that make it to the bottom (likelihood ratio of the evidence), together determine the
                   <em>
                    posterior
                   </em>
                   ratio at the bottom:  3 parts red to 4 parts blue.
                  </p>
                  <h2 class="ng-scope">
                   Test problem
                  </h2>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Here's another Bayesian problem to attempt.  If you successfully solved the earlier problem on your first try, you might try doing this one in your head.
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   10% of widgets are bad and 90% are good.  4% of good widgets emit sparks, and 12% of bad widgets emit sparks.  What percentage of sparking widgets are bad?
                  </p>
                  <div arb-hidden-text="" button-text="Answer" class="ng-scope ng-isolate-scope">
                   <button aria-label="Answer" class="md-primary md-hue-1 md-raised md-button ng-binding ng-scope md-ink-ripple" ng-bind="buttonText" ng-click="toggle()" ng-transclude="" type="button">
                    Answer
                   </button>
                   <div class="hidden-text display-none">
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      There's
                      <span arb-math-compiler="$1%20%3A%209$">
                       <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                        <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-27">
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-28">
                          1
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-29" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-30">
                          9
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <script id="MathJax-Element-3" type="math/tex">
                        1 : 9
                       </script>
                      </span>
                      bad vs. good widgets.  (9 times as many good widgets as bad widgets; widgets are 1/9 as likely to be bad as good.)
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      Bad vs. good widgets have a
                      <span arb-math-compiler="$12%20%3A%204$">
                       <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                        <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-31">
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-32">
                          12
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-33" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-34">
                          4
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <script id="MathJax-Element-4" type="math/tex">
                        12 : 4
                       </script>
                      </span>
                      relative likelihood to spark, which simplifies to
                      <span arb-math-compiler="$3%20%3A%201.$">
                       <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                        <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-35">
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-36">
                          3
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-37" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-38">
                          1.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <script id="MathJax-Element-5" type="math/tex">
                        3 : 1.
                       </script>
                      </span>
                      (Bad widgets are 3 times as likely to emit sparks as good widgets.)
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      <span arb-math-compiler="$(1%20%3A%209)%20%5Ccdot%20(3%20%3A%201)%20%3D%20(3%20%3A%209)%20%5Ccong%20(1%20%3A%203).$">
                       <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                        <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-39">
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-40" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                          (
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-41">
                          1
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-42" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-43">
                          9
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-44" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                          )
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-45" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                          ⋅
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-46" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                          (
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-47">
                          3
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-48" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-49">
                          1
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-50" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                          )
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-51" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                          =
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-52" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                          (
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-53">
                          3
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-54" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-55">
                          9
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-56" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                          )
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-57" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                          ≅
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-58" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                          (
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-59">
                          1
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-60" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-61">
                          3
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-62" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                          )
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-63" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                          .
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <script id="MathJax-Element-6" type="math/tex">
                        (1 : 9) \cdot (3 : 1) = (3 : 9) \cong (1 : 3).
                       </script>
                      </span>
                      (1 bad sparking widget for every 3 good sparking widgets.)
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      Odds of
                      <span arb-math-compiler="$1%20%3A%203$">
                       <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                        <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-64">
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-65">
                          1
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-66" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-67">
                          3
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <script id="MathJax-Element-7" type="math/tex">
                        1 : 3
                       </script>
                      </span>
                      convert to a probability of
                      <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B1%2B3%7D%20%3D%20%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B4%7D%20%3D%2025%5C%25.$">
                       <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                        <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-68">
                         <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-69" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                          <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                           <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-70">
                            1
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                           <span class="MJXp-denom">
                            <span>
                             <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                             </span>
                            </span>
                            <span>
                             <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                              <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-71">
                               1
                              </span>
                              <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-72">
                               +
                              </span>
                              <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-73">
                               3
                              </span>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-74" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                          =
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-75" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                          <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                           <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-76">
                            1
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                           <span class="MJXp-denom">
                            <span>
                             <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                             </span>
                            </span>
                            <span>
                             <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                              <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-77">
                               4
                              </span>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-78" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                          =
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-79">
                          25
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mi" id="MJXp-Span-80">
                          %
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-81" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                          .
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <script id="MathJax-Element-8" type="math/tex">
                        \frac{1}{1+3} = \frac{1}{4} = 25\%.
                       </script>
                      </span>
                      (25% of sparking widgets are bad.)
                     </li>
                    </ul>
                   </div>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                  </div>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   (If you're having trouble using odds ratios to represent uncertainty, see
                   this intro
                   or
                   this page
                   .)
                  </p>
                  <h1 class="ng-scope">
                   General equation and proof
                  </h1>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   To say exactly what we're doing and prove its validity, we need to introduce some notation from
                   probability theory
                   .
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   If
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-82">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-83">
                       X
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-9" type="math/tex">
                     X
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is a proposition,
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20P(X)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-84">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-85">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-86">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-87" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-88">
                       X
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-89" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-10" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb P(X)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   will denote
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-90">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-91">
                       X
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-11" type="math/tex">
                     X
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   's probability, our quantitative degree of belief in
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X.$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-92">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-93">
                       X
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-94" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       .
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-12" type="math/tex">
                     X.
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cneg%20X$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-95">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi" id="MJXp-Span-96">
                       ¬
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-97">
                       X
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-13" type="math/tex">
                     \neg X
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   will denote the negation of
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-98">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-99">
                       X
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-14" type="math/tex">
                     X
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   or the proposition "
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-100">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-101">
                       X
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-15" type="math/tex">
                     X
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is false".
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   If
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-102">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-103">
                       X
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-16" type="math/tex">
                     X
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   and
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$Y$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-104">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-105">
                       Y
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-17" type="math/tex">
                     Y
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   are propositions, then
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X%20%5Cwedge%20Y$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-106">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-107">
                       X
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-108" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                       ∧
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-109">
                       Y
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-18" type="math/tex">
                     X \wedge Y
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   denotes the proposition that both X and Y are true.  Thus
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20P(X%20%5Cwedge%20Y)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-110">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-111">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-112">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-113" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-114">
                       X
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-115" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                       ∧
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-116">
                       Y
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-117" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-19" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb P(X \wedge Y)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   denotes "The probability that
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-118">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-119">
                       X
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-20" type="math/tex">
                     X
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   and
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$Y$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-120">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-121">
                       Y
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-21" type="math/tex">
                     Y
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   are both true."
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   We now define
                   conditional probability
                   :
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%5Cmathbb%20P(X%7CY)%20%3A%3D%20%5Cdfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(X%20%5Cwedge%20Y)%7D%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(Y)%7D%20%20%20%5Ctag*%7B(definition%20of%20conditional%20probability)%7D$$" class="mathjax-div">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math MJXp-display" id="MJXp-Span-122">
                      <span class="MJXp-mtable" id="MJXp-Span-123">
                       <span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mlabeledtr" id="MJXp-Span-124" style="vertical-align: baseline;">
                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-125" style="text-align: center;">
                          <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-126">
                           <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-127">
                            P
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-128" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           (
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-129">
                           X
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-130">
                           <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-131" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                            |
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-132">
                           Y
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-133" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           )
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-134" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                           :=
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mstyle" id="MJXp-Span-135">
                           <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-136" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                            <span class="MJXp-box">
                             <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-137">
                              <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-138">
                               P
                              </span>
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-139" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                              (
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-140">
                              X
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-141" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                              ∧
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-142">
                              Y
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-143" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                              )
                             </span>
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                             <span class="MJXp-denom">
                              <span>
                               <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                               </span>
                              </span>
                              <span>
                               <span class="MJXp-box">
                                <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-144">
                                 <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-145">
                                  P
                                 </span>
                                </span>
                                <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-146" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                                 (
                                </span>
                                <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-147">
                                 Y
                                </span>
                                <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-148" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                                 )
                                </span>
                               </span>
                              </span>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-22" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \mathbb P(X|Y) := \dfrac{\mathbb P(X \wedge Y)}{\mathbb P(Y)}   \tag*{(definition of conditional probability)}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   We pronounce
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20P(X%7CY)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-149">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-150">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-151">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-152" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-153">
                       X
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-154">
                       <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-155" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                        |
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-156">
                       Y
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-157" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-23" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb P(X|Y)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   as "the conditional probability of X, given Y".  Intuitively, this is supposed to mean "The probability that
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$X$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-158">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-159">
                       X
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-24" type="math/tex">
                     X
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is true,
                   <em>
                    assuming
                   </em>
                   that proposition
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$Y$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-160">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-161">
                       Y
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-25" type="math/tex">
                     Y
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is true".
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Defining conditional probability in this way means that to get "the probability that a patient is sick, given that they turned the tongue depressor black" we should put all the sick
                   <em>
                    plus
                   </em>
                   healthy patients with positive test results into a bag, and ask about the probability of drawing a patient who is sick
                   <em>
                    and
                   </em>
                   got a positive test result from that bag.  In other words, we perform the calculation
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cfrac%7B18%7D%7B18%2B24%7D%20%3D%20%5Cfrac%7B3%7D%7B7%7D.$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-162">
                      <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-163" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                       <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-164">
                         18
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                        <span class="MJXp-denom">
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                           <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-165">
                            18
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-166">
                            +
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-167">
                            24
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-168" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                       =
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-169" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                       <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-170">
                         3
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                        <span class="MJXp-denom">
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                           <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-171">
                            7
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-172" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       .
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-26" type="math/tex">
                     \frac{18}{18+24} = \frac{3}{7}.
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <img alt="diseasitis frequency" src="https://i.imgur.com/0XDbrYi.png?0" title=""/>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Rearranging
                   the definition of conditional probability
                   ,
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20P(X%20%5Cwedge%20Y)%20%3D%20%5Cmathbb%20P(Y)%20%5Ccdot%20%5Cmathbb%20P(X%7CY).$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-173">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-174">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-175">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-176" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-177">
                       X
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-178" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                       ∧
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-179">
                       Y
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-180" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-181" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                       =
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-182">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-183">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-184" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-185">
                       Y
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-186" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-187" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                       ⋅
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-188">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-189">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-190" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-191">
                       X
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-192">
                       <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-193" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                        |
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-194">
                       Y
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-195" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-196" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       .
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-27" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb P(X \wedge Y) = \mathbb P(Y) \cdot \mathbb P(X|Y).
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   So to find "the fraction of all patients that are sick
                   <em>
                    and
                   </em>
                   get a positive result", we multiply "the fraction of patients that are sick" times "the probability that a sick patient blackens the tongue depressor".
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   We're now ready to prove Bayes's rule in the form, "the prior odds times the likelihood ratio equals the posterior odds".
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   The "prior odds" is the ratio of sick to healthy patients:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(sick)%7D%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(healthy)%7D%20%20%5Ctag*%7B(prior%20odds)%7D$$" class="mathjax-div">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math MJXp-display" id="MJXp-Span-197">
                      <span class="MJXp-mtable" id="MJXp-Span-198">
                       <span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mlabeledtr" id="MJXp-Span-199" style="vertical-align: baseline;">
                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-200" style="text-align: center;">
                          <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-201" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                           <span class="MJXp-box">
                            <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-202">
                             <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-203">
                              P
                             </span>
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-204" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                             (
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-205">
                             s
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-206">
                             i
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-207">
                             c
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-208">
                             k
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-209" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                             )
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                            <span class="MJXp-denom">
                             <span>
                              <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                              </span>
                             </span>
                             <span>
                              <span class="MJXp-box">
                               <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-210">
                                <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-211">
                                 P
                                </span>
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-212" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                                (
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-213">
                                h
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-214">
                                e
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-215">
                                a
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-216">
                                l
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-217">
                                t
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-218">
                                h
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-219">
                                y
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-220" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                                )
                               </span>
                              </span>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-28" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \frac{\mathbb P(sick)}{\mathbb P(healthy)}  \tag*{(prior odds)}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   The "likelihood ratio" is how much more
                   <em>
                    relatively
                   </em>
                   likely a sick patient is to get a positive test result (turn the tongue depressor black), compared to a healthy patient:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(positive%20%7C%20sick)%7D%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(positive%20%7C%20healthy)%7D%20%5Ctag*%7B(likelihood%20ratio)%7D$$" class="mathjax-div">

                       <span>

                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-224" style="text-align: center;">
                          <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-225" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                           <span class="MJXp-box">
                            <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-226">

                   <em>
                    given
                   </em>
                   that they got a positive test result:
                  </p>

                                p
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-301">
                                o
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-302">
                                s
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-303">
                                i
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-304">
                                t
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-305">
                                i
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-306">
                                v
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-307">
                                e
                               </span>
                               <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-308" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                                )
                               </span>
                              </span>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-30" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \frac{\mathbb P(sick | positive)}{\mathbb P(healthy | positive)} \tag*{(posterior odds)}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Bayes's theorem asserts that
                   <em>
                    prior odds times likelihood ratio equals posterior odds:
                   </em>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(sick)%7D%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(healthy)%7D%20%5Ccdot%20%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(positive%20%7C%20sick)%7D%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(positive%20%7C%20healthy)%7D%20%3D%20%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(sick%20%7C%20positive)%7D%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(healthy%20%7C%20positive)%7D$$" class="mathjax-div">

                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-31" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \frac{\mathbb P(sick)}{\mathbb P(healthy)} \cdot \frac{\mathbb P(positive | sick)}{\mathbb P(positive | healthy)} = \frac{\mathbb P(sick | positive)}{\mathbb P(healthy | positive)}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   We will show this by proving the general form of Bayes's Rule.  For any two hypotheses
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$H_j$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-412">
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-413">

                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-415" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        j
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-32" type="math/tex">
                     H_j
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   and
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$H_k$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-416">
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-417">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-418" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-419" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        k
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-33" type="math/tex">
                     H_k
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   and any piece of new evidence
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$e_0$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-420">
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-421">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-422" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        e
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-423" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        0
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-34" type="math/tex">
                     e_0
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   :
                  </p>

                       <span class="MJXp-box">

                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-440" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">

                      </span>

                    <script id="MathJax-Element-35" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \frac{\mathbb P(H_j)}{\mathbb P(H_k)}
\cdot
\frac{\mathbb P(e_0 | H_j)}{\mathbb P(e_0 | H_k)}
=
\frac{\mathbb P(e_0 \wedge H_j)}{\mathbb P(e_0 \wedge H_k)}
= 
\frac{\mathbb P(e_0 \wedge H_j)/\mathbb P(e_0)}{\mathbb P(e_0 \wedge H_k)/\mathbb P(e_0)}
= 
\frac{\mathbb P(H_j | e_0)}{\mathbb P(H_k | e_0)}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   In the Diseasitis example, this corresponds to performing the operations:
                  </p>
