                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-577">
                            <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-578" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.111em;">
                             /
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-579">
                            0.42
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-580" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                       =
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-581" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                       <span class="MJXp-box">
                        <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-582">
                         0.43
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                        <span class="MJXp-denom">
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-box">
                           <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-583">
                            0.57
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-36" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \frac{0.20}{0.80}
\cdot
\frac{0.90}{0.30}
=
\frac{0.18}{0.24}
= 
\frac{0.18/0.42}{0.24/0.42}
= 
\frac{0.43}{0.57}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Using red for sick, blue for healthy, grey for a mix of sick and healthy patients, and + signs for positive test results, the proof above can be visualized as follows:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <img alt="bayes venn" src="https://i.imgur.com/YBc2nYo.png?0" title=""/>
                  </p>
                  <h2 class="ng-scope">
                   Bayes' theorem
                  </h2>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   An alternative form, sometimes called "Bayes' theorem" to distinguish it from "Bayes' rule" (although not everyone follows this convention), uses absolute probabilities instead of ratios.  The
                   law of marginal probability
                   states that for any set of
                   mutually exclusive and exhaustive
                   possibilities
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5C%7BX_1%2C%20X_2%2C%20...%2C%20X_i%5C%7D$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-584">
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-585" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       {
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-586">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-587" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        X
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-588" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        1
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-589" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       ,
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-590">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-591" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        X
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-592" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        2
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-593" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       ,
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-594" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       .
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-595" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       .
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-596" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       .
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-597" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       ,
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-598">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-599" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        X
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-600" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        i
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-601" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       }
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-37" type="math/tex">
                     \{X_1, X_2, ..., X_i\}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   and any proposition
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$Y$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-602">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-603">
                       Y
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-38" type="math/tex">
                     Y
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   :
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%5Cmathbb%20P(Y)%20%3D%20%5Csum_i%20%5Cmathbb%20P(Y%20%5Cwedge%20X_i)%20%20%20%5Ctag*%7B(law%20of%20marginal%20probability)%7D$$" class="mathjax-div">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math MJXp-display" id="MJXp-Span-604">
                      <span class="MJXp-mtable" id="MJXp-Span-605">
                       <span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mlabeledtr" id="MJXp-Span-606" style="vertical-align: baseline;">
                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-607" style="text-align: center;">
                          <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-608">
                           <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-609">
                            P
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-610" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           (
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-611">
                           Y
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-612" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           )
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-613" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                           =
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-munderover" id="MJXp-Span-614">
                           <span class="">
                            <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-615" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                             <span class="MJXp-largeop">
                              ∑
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-script">
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-616" style="margin-left: 0px;">
                             i
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-617">
                           <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-618">
                            P
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-619" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           (
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-620">
                           Y
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-621" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                           ∧
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-622">
                           <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-623" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                            X
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-624" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                            i
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-625" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           )
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-39" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \mathbb P(Y) = \sum_i \mathbb P(Y \wedge X_i)   \tag*{(law of marginal probability)}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Then we can derive an expression for the absolute (non-relative) probability of a proposition
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$H_k$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-626">
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-627">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-628" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-629" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        k
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-40" type="math/tex">
                     H_k
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   after observing evidence
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$e_0$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-630">
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-631">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-632" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        e
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-633" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        0
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-41" type="math/tex">
                     e_0
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   as follows:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%0A%5Cmathbb%20P(H_k%20%7C%20e_0)%0A%3D%20%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(H_k%20%5Cwedge%20e_0)%7D%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(e_0)%7D%0A%3D%20%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(e_0%20%5Cwedge%20H_k)%7D%7B%5Csum_i%20P(e_0%20%5Cwedge%20H_i)%7D%0A%3D%20%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(e_0%20%7C%20X_k)%20%5Ccdot%20%5Cmathbb%20P(X_k)%7D%7B%5Csum_i%20%5Cmathbb%20P(e_0%20%7C%20X_i)%20%5Ccdot%20%5Cmathbb%20P(X_i)%7D%0A$$" class="mathjax-div">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math MJXp-display" id="MJXp-Span-634">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-635">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-636">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-637" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-638">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-639" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-640" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        k
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-641">
                       <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-642" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                        |
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-643">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-644" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        e
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-645" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">

                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-646" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">

                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-648" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                       <span class="MJXp-box">

                         </span>

                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-651" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">

                         <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-654" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">

                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-656">

                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-659" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">

                       <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                        <span class="MJXp-denom">
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">

                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-708">
                         <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-709">

                         </span>
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-710" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                         (
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-711">
                         <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-712" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                          X
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-713" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                          k
                         </span>
                        </span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-714" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                         )
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                        <span class="MJXp-denom">
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span>
                          <span class="MJXp-box">
                           <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-715">
                            <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-716" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                             ∑
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-717" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                             i
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-718">
                            <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-719">
                             P
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-720" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                            (
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-721">
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-722" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                             e
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-723" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                             0
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-724">
                            <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-725" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                             |
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-726">
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-727" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                             X
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-728" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                             i
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-729" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                            )
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-730" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                            ⋅
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-731">
                            <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-732">
                             P
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-733" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                            (
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-734">
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-735" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                             X
                            </span>
                            <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-736" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                             i
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-737" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                            )
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-42" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \mathbb P(H_k | e_0)
= \frac{\mathbb P(H_k \wedge e_0)}{\mathbb P(e_0)}
= \frac{\mathbb P(e_0 \wedge H_k)}{\sum_i P(e_0 \wedge H_i)}
= \frac{\mathbb P(e_0 | X_k) \cdot \mathbb P(X_k)}{\sum_i \mathbb P(e_0 | X_i) \cdot \mathbb P(X_i)}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   The equation of the first and last terms above is what you will usually see described as Bayes' theorem.
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   To see why this decomposition might be useful, note that
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20P(sick%20%7C%20positive)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-738">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-739">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-740">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-741" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-742">
                       s
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-743">
                       i
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-744">
                       c
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-745">
                       k
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-746">
                       <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-747" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                        |
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-748">
                       p
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-749">
                       o
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-750">
                       s
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-751">
                       i
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-752">
                       t
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-753">
                       i
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-754">
                       v
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-755">
                       e
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-756" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-43" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb P(sick | positive)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is an
                   <em>
                    inferential
                   </em>
                   step, a conclusion that we make after observing a new piece of evidence.
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20P(positive%20%7C%20sick)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-757">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-758">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-759">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-760" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-761">
                       p
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-762">
                       o
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-763">
                       s
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-764">
                       i
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-765">
                       t
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-766">
                       i
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-767">
                       v
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-768">
                       e
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-769">
                       <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-770" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                        |
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-771">
                       s
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-772">
                       i
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-773">
                       c
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-774">
                       k
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-775" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-44" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb P(positive | sick)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is a piece of
                   <em>
                    causal
                   </em>
                   information we are likely to have on hand, for example by testing groups of sick patients to see how many of them turn the tongue depressor black.
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20P(sick)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-776">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-777">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-778">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-779" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-780">
                       s
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-781">
                       i
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-782">
                       c
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-783">
                       k
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-784" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-45" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb P(sick)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   describes our state of belief before making any new observations.  So Bayes' theorem can be seen as taking what we already believe about the world (including our prior belief about how different imaginable states of affairs would generate different observations), plus an actual observation, and outputting a new state of belief about the world.
                  </p>
                  <h2 class="ng-scope">
                   Vector and functional generalizations
                  </h2>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Since the proof of Bayes' rule holds for
                   <em>
                    any pair
                   </em>
                   of hypotheses, it also holds for relative belief in any number of hypotheses.  Furthermore, we can repeatedly multiply by likelihood ratios to chain together any number of pieces of evidence.
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Suppose there's a bathtub full of coins:
                  </p>
                  <ul class="ng-scope">
                   <li>
                    Half the coins are "fair" and have a 50% probability of coming up Heads each time they are thrown.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    A third of the coins are biased to produce Heads 25% of the time (Tails 75%).
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    The remaining sixth of the coins are biased to produce Heads 75% of the time.
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   You randomly draw a coin, flip it three times, and get the result
                   <strong>
                    HTH
                   </strong>
                   .  What's the chance this is a fair coin?
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   We can validly calculate the answer as follows:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%0A%5Cbegin%7Barray%7D%7Brll%7D%0A%20%20%26%20(3%20%3A%202%20%3A%201)%20%26%20%5Ccong%20(%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%20%3A%20%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B3%7D%20%3A%20%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B6%7D)%20%5C%5C%0A%5Ctimes%20%26%20(2%20%3A%201%20%3A%203)%20%26%20%5Ccong%20(%20%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%20%3A%20%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B4%7D%20%3A%20%5Cfrac%7B3%7D%7B4%7D%20)%20%5C%5C%0A%5Ctimes%20%26%20(2%20%3A%203%20%3A%201)%20%26%20%5Ccong%20(%20%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%20%3A%20%5Cfrac%7B3%7D%7B4%7D%20%3A%20%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B4%7D%20)%20%5C%5C%0A%5Ctimes%20%26%20(2%20%3A%201%20%3A%203)%20%26%20%5C%5C%0A%3D%20%26%20(24%20%3A%206%20%3A%209)%20%26%20%5Ccong%20(8%20%3A%202%20%3A%203)%20%5Ccong%20(%5Cfrac%7B8%7D%7B13%7D%20%3A%20%5Cfrac%7B2%7D%7B13%7D%20%3A%20%5Cfrac%7B3%7D%7B13%7D)%0A%5Cend%7Barray%7D%0A$$" class="mathjax-div">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math MJXp-display" id="MJXp-Span-785">
                      <span class="MJXp-mtable" id="MJXp-Span-786">
                       <span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mtr" id="MJXp-Span-787" style="vertical-align: baseline;">
                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-788" style="text-align: right;">
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-789" style="padding-left: 1em; text-align: left;">
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-790" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           (
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-791">
                           3
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-792" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                           :
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-793">
                           2
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-794" style="margin-left: 0.111em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                           :
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-795">
                           1
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-796" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           )
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-797" style="padding-left: 1em; text-align: left;">
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-798" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                           ≅
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-799" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           (
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-800" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">

                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-822" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           )
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-823" style="padding-left: 1em; padding-top: 0.4em; text-align: left;">
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-824" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">
                           ≅
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-825" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           (
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-826" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">

                            <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-827">

                             <span>

                             2
                            </span>

                            <span class="MJXp-denom">

                           :
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-906" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                           <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                            <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-907">
                             3
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                            <span class="MJXp-denom">
                             <span>
                              <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                              </span>
                             </span>
                             <span>
                              <span class="MJXp-box MJXp-script">
                               <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-908">
                                13
                               </span>
                              </span>
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-909" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           )
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-46" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \begin{array}{rll}
  & (3 : 2 : 1) & \cong (\frac{1}{2} : \frac{1}{3} : \frac{1}{6}) \\
\times & (2 : 1 : 3) & \cong ( \frac{1}{2} : \frac{1}{4} : \frac{3}{4} ) \\
\times & (2 : 3 : 1) & \cong ( \frac{1}{2} : \frac{3}{4} : \frac{1}{4} ) \\
\times & (2 : 1 : 3) & \\
= & (24 : 6 : 9) & \cong (8 : 2 : 3) \cong (\frac{8}{13} : \frac{2}{13} : \frac{3}{13})
\end{array}
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   So the posterior probability the coin is fair is 8/13 or ~62%.
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   This is one reason it's good to know the
                   odds form
                   of Bayes' rule, not just the
                   probability form
                   in which Bayes' theorem is often given.
                   <span arb-text-popover-anchor="" class="markdown-note ng-isolate-scope" encoded-html="Imagine%20trying%20to%20do%20the%20above%20calculation%20by%20repeatedly%20applying%20the%20form%20of%20the%20theorem%20that%20says%3A%20%3Cspan%20class%3D%22mathjax-div%22%20arb-math-compiler%3D%22%24%24%255Cmathbb%2520P(H_k%2520%257C%2520e_0)%2520%253D%2520%255Cfrac%257B%255Cmathbb%2520P(e_0%2520%257C%2520X_k)%2520%255Ccdot%2520%255Cmathbb%2520P(X_k)%257D%257B%255Csum_i%2520%255Cmathbb%2520P(e_o%2520%257C%2520X_i)%2520%255Ccdot%2520%255Cmathbb%2520P(X_i)%257D%24%24%22%3E%26nbsp%3B%3C%2Fspan%3E%20" replacement-text="3">
                    3
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   We can generalize further by writing Bayes' rule in a functional form.  If
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20O(H_i)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-910">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-911">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-912">
                        O
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-913" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-914">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-915" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-916" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        i
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-917" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-47" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb O(H_i)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is a relative belief vector or relative belief function on the variable
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$H%2C$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-918">
                      <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-919">
                       H
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-920" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       ,
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-48" type="math/tex">
                     H,
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   and
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathcal%20L(e_0%20%7C%20H_i)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-921">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-922">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-cal" id="MJXp-Span-923">
                        L
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-924" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-925">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-926" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        e
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-927" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        0
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-928">
                       <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-929" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                        |
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-930">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-931" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-932" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        i
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-933" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-49" type="math/tex">
                     \mathcal L(e_0 | H_i)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is the likelihood function giving the relative chance of observing evidence
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$e_0$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-934">
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-935">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-936" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        e
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-937" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        0
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-50" type="math/tex">
                     e_0
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   given each possible state of affairs
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$H_i%2C$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-938">
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-939">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-940" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-941" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        i
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-942" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.222em;">
                       ,
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-51" type="math/tex">
                     H_i,
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   then relative posterior belief
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20O(H_i%20%7C%20e_0)$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-943">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-944">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-945">
                        O
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-946" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-947">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-948" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-949" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        i
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-950">
                       <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-951" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                        |
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-952">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-953" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        e
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-954" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        0
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-955" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-52" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb O(H_i | e_0)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   is given by:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%5Cmathbb%20O(H_i%20%7C%20e_0)%20%3D%20%5Cmathcal%20L(e_0%20%7C%20H_i)%20%5Ccdot%20%5Cmathbb%20O(H_i)$$" class="mathjax-div">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math MJXp-display" id="MJXp-Span-956">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-957">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-958">
                        O
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-959" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-960">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-961" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-962" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">

                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-963">
                       <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-964" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                        |
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-965">

                       <span class="MJXp-mn MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-967" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">

                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-968" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">

                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-969" style="margin-left: 0.333em; margin-right: 0.333em;">

                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-970">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-cal" id="MJXp-Span-971">

                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-972" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">

                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-973">

                        |
                       </span>

                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-978">

                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-980" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">

                       </span>

                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-982" style="margin-left: 0.267em; margin-right: 0.267em;">
                       ⋅
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-983">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-984">
                        O
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-985" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       (
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-986">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-987" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                        H
                       </span>
                       <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-988" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">
                        i
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-989" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                       )
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-53" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \mathbb O(H_i | e_0) = \mathcal L(e_0 | H_i) \cdot \mathbb O(H_i)
                    </script>
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   If we
                   normalize
                   the relative odds
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20O$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-990">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-991">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-992">
                        O
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-54" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb O
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   into absolute probabilities
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20P$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-993">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-994">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-995">
                        P
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-55" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb P
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   - that is, divide through
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$%5Cmathbb%20O$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-996">
                      <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-997">
                       <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-998">
                        O
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-56" type="math/tex">
                     \mathbb O
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   by its sum or integral so that the new function sums or integrates to
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$1$">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math" id="MJXp-Span-999">
                      <span class="MJXp-mn" id="MJXp-Span-1000">
                       1
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <script id="MathJax-Element-57" type="math/tex">
                     1
                    </script>
                   </span>
                   - then we obtain Bayes' rule for probability functions:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   <span arb-math-compiler="$$%5Cmathbb%20P(H_i%20%7C%20e_0)%20%5Cpropto%20%5Cmathcal%20L(e_0%20%7C%20H_i)%20%5Ccdot%20%5Cmathbb%20P(H_i)%20%20%5Ctag*%7B(functional%20form%20of%20Bayes'%20rule)%7D$$" class="mathjax-div">
                    <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                     <span class="MJXp-math MJXp-display" id="MJXp-Span-1001">
                      <span class="MJXp-mtable" id="MJXp-Span-1002">
                       <span>
                        <span class="MJXp-mlabeledtr" id="MJXp-Span-1003" style="vertical-align: baseline;">
                         <span class="MJXp-mtd" id="MJXp-Span-1004" style="text-align: center;">

                            P

                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-1007" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">

                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-1008">
                           <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic" id="MJXp-Span-1009" style="margin-right: 0.05em;">
                            H
                           </span>
                           <span class="MJXp-mi MJXp-italic MJXp-script" id="MJXp-Span-1010" style="vertical-align: -0.4em;">

                            |

                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-msubsup" id="MJXp-Span-1013">

                    <script id="MathJax-Element-58" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                     \mathbb P(H_i | e_0) \propto \mathcal L(e_0 | H_i) \cdot \mathbb P(H_i)  \tag*{(functional form of Bayes' rule)}
                    </script>

                  </p>
                  <h1 class="ng-scope">
                   Applications of Bayesian reasoning
                  </h1>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   This general Bayesian framework - prior belief, evidence, posterior belief - is a lens through which we can view a
                   <em>
                    lot
                   </em>
                   of formal and informal reasoning plus a large amount of entirely nonverbal cognitive-ish phenomena.
                   <span arb-text-popover-anchor="" class="markdown-note ng-isolate-scope" encoded-html="This%20broad%20statement%20is%20widely%20agreed.%20%20Exactly%20%3Cem%3Ewhich%3C%2Fem%3E%20phenomena%20are%20good%20to%20view%20through%20a%20Bayesian%20lens%20is%20sometimes%20disputed." replacement-text="4">
                    4
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Examples of people who might want to study Bayesian reasoning include:
                  </p>
                  <ul class="ng-scope">
                   <li>
                    Professionals who use statistics, such as scientists or medical doctors.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Computer programmers working in the field of machine learning.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Human beings trying to think.
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   The third application is probably of the widest general interest.
                  </p>
                  <h2 class="ng-scope">
                   Example human applications of Bayesian reasoning
                  </h2>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   Philip Tetlock found when studying "superforecasters", people who were especially good at predicting future events:
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   "The superforecasters are a numerate bunch: many know about Bayes' theorem and could deploy it if they felt it was worth the trouble. But they rarely crunch the numbers so explicitly. What matters far more to the superforecasters than Bayes' theorem is Bayes' core insight of gradually getting closer to the truth by constantly updating in proportion to the weight of the evidence." — Philip Tetlock and Dan Gardner,
                   Superforecasting
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   This is some evidence that
                   <em>
                    knowing about
                   </em>
                   Bayes' rule and understanding its
                   <em>
                    qualitative
                   </em>
                   implications is a factor in delivering better-than-average intuitive human reasoning.  This pattern is illustrated in the next couple of examples.
                  </p>
                  <h3 class="ng-scope">
                   The OKCupid date.
                  </h3>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   One realistic example of Bayesian reasoning was deployed by one of the early test volunteers for a much earlier version of a guide to Bayes' rule.  She had scheduled a date with a 96% OKCupid match, who had then cancelled that date without other explanation.  After spending some mental time bouncing back and forth between "that doesn't seem like a good sign" versus "maybe there was a good reason he canceled", she decided to try looking at the problem using that Bayes thing she'd just learned about.  She estimated:
                  </p>
                  <ul class="ng-scope">
                   <li>
                    A 96% OKCupid match like this one, had prior odds of 2 : 5 for being a desirable versus undesirable date.  (Based on her prior experience with 96% OKCupid matches, and the details of his profile.)
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Men she doesn't want to go out with are 3 times as likely as men she might want to go out with to cancel a first date without other explanation.
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   This implied posterior odds of 2 : 15 that this was an undesirable date, which was unfavorable enough not to pursue him further.
                   <span arb-text-popover-anchor="" class="markdown-note ng-isolate-scope" encoded-html="She%20sent%20him%20what%20might%20very%20well%20have%20been%20the%20first%20explicitly%20Bayesian%20rejection%20notice%20in%20dating%20history%2C%20reasoning%20that%20if%20he%20wrote%20back%20with%20a%20Bayesian%20counterargument%2C%20this%20would%20promote%20him%20to%20being%20interesting%20again.%20%20He%20didn't%20write%20back." replacement-text="5">
                    5
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   The point of looking at the problem this way is not that she knew
                   <em>
                    exact
                   </em>
                   probabilities and could calculate that the man had an exactly 88% chance of being undesirable.  Rather, by breaking up the problem in that way, she was able to summarize what she thought she knew in compact form, see what those beliefs already implied, and stop bouncing back and forth between imagined reasons why a good date might cancel versus reasons to protect herself from potential bad dates.  An answer
                   <em>
                    roughly
                   </em>
                   in the range of 15/17 made the decision clear.
                  </p>
                  <h3 class="ng-scope">
                   Internment of Japanese-Americans during World War II
                  </h3>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   From Robyn Dawes's
                   Rational Choice in an Uncertain World
                   :
                  </p>
                  <blockquote class="ng-scope">
                   <p>
                    Post-hoc fitting of evidence to hypothesis was involved in a most grievous chapter in United States history: the internment of Japanese-Americans at the beginning of the Second World War.  When California governor Earl Warren testified before a congressional hearing in San Francisco on February 21, 1942, a questioner pointed out that there had been no sabotage or any other type of espionage by the Japanese-Americans up to that time.  Warren responded, "I take the view that this lack
                    subversive activity
                    is the most ominous sign in our whole situation. It convinces me more than perhaps any other factor that the sabotage we are to get, the Fifth Column activities are to get, are timed just like Pearl Harbor was timed... I believe we are just being lulled into a false sense of security."
                   </p>
                  </blockquote>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   You might want to take your own shot at guessing what Dawes had to say about a Bayesian view of this situation, before reading further.
                  </p>
                  <div arb-hidden-text="" button-text="Answer" class="ng-scope ng-isolate-scope">
                   <button aria-label="Answer" class="md-primary md-hue-1 md-raised md-button ng-binding ng-scope md-ink-ripple" ng-bind="buttonText" ng-click="toggle()" ng-transclude="" type="button">
                    Answer
                   </button>
                   <div class="hidden-text display-none">
                    <p>
                     Suppose we put ourselves into the shoes of this congressional hearing, and imagine ourselves trying to set up this problem.
                    </p>
                    <ul>
                     <li>
                      The
                      prior
                      odds
                      that there would be a conspiracy of Japanese-American saboteurs.
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      The
                      likelihood
                      of the observation "no visible sabotage or any other type of espionage",
                      <em>
                       given
                      </em>
                      that a Fifth Column actually existed.
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      The likelihood of the observation "no visible sabotage from Japanese-Americans", in the possible world where there is
                      <em>
                       no
                      </em>
                      such conspiracy.
                     </li>
                    </ul>
                    <p>
                     As soon as we set up this problem, we realize that, whatever the probability of "no sabotage" being observed if there is a conspiracy, the likelihood of observing "no sabotage" if there
                     <em>
                      isn't
                     </em>
                     a conspiracy must be even higher.  This means that the likelihood ratio:
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     <span arb-math-compiler="$$%5Cfrac%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(%5Cneg%20%5Ctext%7Bsabotage%7D%20%7C%20%5Ctext%20%7Bconspiracy%7D)%7D%7B%5Cmathbb%20P(%5Cneg%20%5Ctext%20%7Bsabotage%7D%20%7C%20%5Cneg%20%5Ctext%20%7Bconspiracy%7D)%7D$$" class="mathjax-div">
                      <span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;">
                       <span class="MJXp-math MJXp-display" id="MJXp-Span-1038">
                        <span class="MJXp-mfrac" id="MJXp-Span-1039" style="vertical-align: 0.25em;">
                         <span class="MJXp-box">
                          <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-1040">
                           <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-1041">
                            P
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-1042" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           (
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mi" id="MJXp-Span-1043">
                           ¬
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mtext" id="MJXp-Span-1044">
                           sabotage
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-1045">
                           <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-1046" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                            |
                           </span>
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mtext" id="MJXp-Span-1047">
                           conspiracy
                          </span>
                          <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-1048" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                           )
                          </span>
                         </span>
                         <span class="MJXp-box" style="margin-top: -0.9em;">
                          <span class="MJXp-denom">
                           <span>
                            <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span>
                            <span class="MJXp-box">
                             <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-1049">
                              <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-1050">
                               P
                              </span>
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-1051" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                              (
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mi" id="MJXp-Span-1052">
                              ¬
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mtext" id="MJXp-Span-1053">
                              sabotage
                             </span>

                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <script id="MathJax-Element-59" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                       \frac{\mathbb P(\neg \text{sabotage} | \text {conspiracy})}{\mathbb P(\neg \text {sabotage} | \neg \text {conspiracy})}
                      </script>
                     </span>
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     ...must be
                     <em>
                      less than 1,
                     </em>
                     and accordingly:
                    </p>
                    <p>

                          <span class="MJXp-denom">
                           <span>
                            <span class="MJXp-rule" style="height: 1em; border-top: none; border-bottom: 1px solid; margin: 0.1em 0px;">
                            </span>
                           </span>
                           <span>
                            <span class="MJXp-box">
                             <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-1104">
                              <span class="MJXp-mi undefined" id="MJXp-Span-1105">
                               P
                              </span>
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-1106" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                              (
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mi" id="MJXp-Span-1107">
                              ¬
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mtext" id="MJXp-Span-1108">
                              sabotage
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mrow" id="MJXp-Span-1109">
                              <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-1110" style="margin-left: 0.167em; margin-right: 0.167em;">
                               |
                              </span>
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mi" id="MJXp-Span-1111">
                              ¬
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mtext" id="MJXp-Span-1112">
                              conspiracy
                             </span>
                             <span class="MJXp-mo" id="MJXp-Span-1113" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                              )
                             </span>
                            </span>
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <script id="MathJax-Element-60" type="math/tex; mode=display">
                       \frac{\mathbb P(\text {conspiracy} | \neg \text{sabotage})}{\mathbb P(\neg \text {conspiracy} | \neg \text{sabotage})}
<
\frac{\mathbb P(\text {conspiracy})}{\mathbb P(\neg \text {conspiracy})}
\cdot
\frac{\mathbb P(\neg \text{sabotage} | \text {conspiracy})}{\mathbb P(\neg \text {sabotage} | \neg \text {conspiracy})}
                      </script>
                     </span>
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     Observing the total absence of any sabotage can only decrease our estimate that there's a Japanese-American Fifth Column, not increase it.  (It definitely shouldn't be "the most ominous" sign that convinces us "more than any other factor" that the Fifth Column exists.)
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     Again, what matters is not the
                     <em>
                      exact
                     </em>
                     likelihood of observing no sabotage given that a Fifth Column actually exists.  As soon as we set up the Bayesian problem, we can see there's something
                     <em>
                      qualitatively
                     </em>
                     wrong with Earl Warren's reasoning.
                    </p>
                   </div>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                  </div>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                  </p>
                  <h1 class="ng-scope">
                   Further reading
                  </h1>
                  <p class="ng-scope">
                   This has been a very brief and high-speed presentation of Bayes and Bayesianism.  It should go without saying that a vast literature, nay, a universe of literature, exists on Bayesian statistical methods and Bayesian epistemology and Bayesian algorithms in machine learning.  Staying inside Arbital, you might be interested in moving on to read:
                  </p>
                  <h2 class="ng-scope">
                   More on the technical side of Bayes' rule
                  </h2>
                  <ul class="ng-scope">
                   <li>
                    A sadly short list of
                    example Bayesian word problems
                    .  Want to add more?  (Hint hint.)
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Bayes' rule: Proportional form.
                    The fastest way to present a step in Bayesian reasoning in a way that will sound sort of understandable to somebody who's never heard of Bayes.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Bayes' rule: Log-odds form.
                    A simple transformation of Bayes' rule reveals tools for measuring degree of belief, and strength of evidence.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    The "Naive Bayes" algorithm.
                    (Scroll down to the middle.)  The original simple Bayesian spam filter.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Non-naive multiple updates.
                    (Scroll down past Naive Bayes.)  How to avoid double-counting the evidence, or worse, when considering multiple items of
                    <em>
                     correlated
                    </em>
                    evidence.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Laplace's Rule of Succession.
                    The classic example of an
                    inductive prior
                    .
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                  <h2 class="ng-scope">
                   More on intuitive implications of Bayes' rule
                  </h2>
                  <ul class="ng-scope">
                   <li>
                    A Bayesian view of scientific virtues.
                    Why is it that science relies on bold, precise, and falsifiable predictions? Because of Bayes' rule, of course.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Update by inches.
                    It's virtuous to change your mind in response to overwhelming evidence. It's even more virtuous to shift your beliefs a little bit at a time, in response to
                    <em>
                     all
                    </em>
                    evidence (no matter how small).
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Belief revision as probability elimination.
                    Update your beliefs by throwing away large chunks of probability mass.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Shift towards the hypothesis of least surprise.
                    When you see new evidence, ask: which hypothesis is
                    <em>
                     least surprised?
                    </em>
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Extraordinary claims require extraordinary evidence.
                    The people who adamantly claim they were abducted by aliens do provide
                    <em>
                     some
                    </em>
                    evidence for aliens. They just don't provide quantitatively
                    <em>
                     enough
                    </em>
                    evidence.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Ideal reasoning via Bayes' rule.
                    Bayes' rule is to reasoning as the
                    Carnot cycle
                    is to engines: Nobody can be a perfect Bayesian, but Bayesian reasoning is still the theoretical ideal.
                   </li>
                   <li>
                    Likelihoods, p-values, and the replication crisis.
                    Arguably, a large part of the replication crisis can ultimately be traced back to the way journals treat p-values, and a large number of those problems can be summed up as "P-values are not Bayesian."
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </arb-markdown>
